[30;1m4 | [0m[35mclass NoValue(Resolver):[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35m    """This resolver resolves to nothing, functioning just like the AWS::NoValue special value. When[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35m    assigned to a resolvable Stack property, it will remove the config key/value from the stack or[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35m    the container on the stack where it has been assigned, as if this value wasn't assigned at all.[0m
